<Gmap_id>0x80960d967cbef955:0x7b91bd138cc09158< /Gmap_id>< Review>
My family and I were in need of breakfast before heading back home. The Warming Hut was probably the best breakfast location I have ever been to. The environment of the restaurant was lively and extremely comforting. The aesthetic themes they chose for their walls to the cute red coffee cups really give off this warm, welcoming feeling that really compliment the cold snowy location.

The staff are amazing, they are very polite and friendly. They greeted us with smiles and made it our satisfaction their priority. All of them seemed to love their job and the manager knows exactly how to treat everyone.

I had the chorizo omelette, and my uncle had the monkey cakes. The monkey cakes were humongous and were stuffed with chocolate, bananas, and topped off with a generous amount of whipped cream. He found it perfect, but I thought there was too much chocolate and not enough cake. The chorizo omelette was delicious. The chefs behind the dish really knew what to add to make the spicy sausage even more scrumptious.</Review>

< review>
There are reviews stating the wait time is long. I would like to state that this restuarant is new. When you first open a business you have to work out the kinks.

I ordered an ice tea, bowl of creamy tomatoe soup with a grilled cheese and a ceaser salad. I think the tomatoe soup was probably the best tomatoe soup I have had in a long while.

Ceaser salad was done well, good homemade dressing, homemade croutons, and shredded romaine the way I like it.

The grilled cheese was on a good loaf of bread.

I really enjoy the outdoor seating and decor. Use of mason jars for glasses and nice dishwear for the food.

The owner is also very polite and you can tell she takes pride in her business and wants her customers to enjoy themselves.

If you are in town give them a chance!<//review>

< review>
We were desperate out-of-towners visiting the area for less than one week.   We needed help, and needed it fast! <Date>1446586038047< /Date><rate>5< /rate><review>Home away from home. My family rescues pets with special needs, and Dr Garcia and staff have provided excellent and affordable pet care. We were recommended through first grade teacher who also rescues animals, and let me assure you on Family Dog and Cat Hospital's high standards. This clean, modern, airy, friendly clinic also offers 'hospital stays' (boarding) which costs about the same as day care centers but the added perk is that your pet has a professional, licensed doctor on call, your pet gets walked twice daily across street at Library Park. And, as a special bonus, if you have your pet groomed on same day you return from travel, that day's boarding fee is waived.

While my family is allergic to cats, when one tiny kitten was trapped in a car engine and police pulled him out, Dr Garcia and crew took him in, healed him, and by third day we adopted him because he was too affectionate and adorable. Our kitty had sweetness in him but was previously covered in oil and a rawring hissy fit, but thanks to staff member Rod wearing kitty all over the clinic, this hissball of fear turned into the coolest cat, and now he's our specially buddy, Claritin and all. After kitty reached six months, he was spayed easy breezy, and we got a discount for being returning clients.

Something else........ We've also had to euthanize our elderly, dying dogs. Family Dog & Cat Hospital offers respectable, loving services. Our very old and sick dog was euthanized in our front yard, on the lawn during the morning with birds and nature, all the things our dog loved as she passed away peacefully and ethically. And in being kind people, Dr Garcia, Dave and Roxy wrapped our doggy up and carried her away. A few weeks later, our dog's remains were placed in a lovely cedar box with brass lock, her name engraved on plate, (welling up now) her paw print in plaster of Paris keepsake dish, and lock of her fur.... things I could not think to do at the time our dog was dying, but it was so comforting to receive these treasures from our dog, that it this kindness sealed the deal with our appreciation for Family Dog & Cat Hospital.

and now my cat will type the rest of his message:  "m,iijiuduydryfgfrB" which means "I love Family Dog and Cat Hospital."

PS: This is the ONLY place in town that will trim our dogs' and kitty's nails.... our pets freak out when groomed elsewhere but at least with Family Dog & Cat Hospital, it's FULL SERVICE.

PSS: Dr Garcia is A LADY, not a male vet, so perhaps previous poster is thinking of Dr White because my family was ripped off there for sure, and that was a male vet in Monrovia (not many in town). Just sayin'< /review>< pictures>

<GmapID>0x80dbd00c0270e4cf:0x8e7a93f1db56deee< /GmapID><Review>So enchanting!

I'm crazy about afternoon tea. If I could I'd have a tea party every single day!

The ladies here are simply the sweetest and have major skills in the kitchen. Everything I've ever tried here was absolutely delicious.

Maybe my man and I were on a mountain high on our most recent visit but we keep talking about our time here. And how many men do you know that are down for a tea party? I was taking a chance when I surprised him with reservations here but he loved everything nearly as much as I did.

This historic place was once a home to a gold
miner that was built in 1898. Can you imagine all the things that have gone on here?

There are hundreds of different teas to choose from and several different tea party experiences. I always go for the cottage classic because it's the most elaborate and so worth it. What you can expect is delicious seasonal soup, an assortment of finger sandwiches, scones with all sorts of toppings from jam & cream, and lots of tiny desserts! Each guest may also choose their favorite tea.

You can also purchase teas to-go both bagged or loose, gorgeous china, antique items, books, and many different types of gifts for tea lovers.

*During COVID your tea service will be in their gorgeous garden instead of in the house.<//Review><user>106447694604539697362<//user><Time>1608511561966<//Time><user_name>Ania K<//user_name><Pictures>None</Pictures></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
One of my favorite places to visit when I'm in Julian. They have the largest selection of teas I have ever seen. They also have quite a selection of tea and kitchen related items. The building itself is quite interesting. It's an over one hundred year old rickety Victorian that is fun to roam around in and is supposedly haunted. Go stick your pinky out and pretend you're English for an hour. It's probably best to make a reservation since this place is popular.</Review>

<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
I finally had tea here during my last stay in Julian! It was well worth it. I was lucky enough to get a walk in afternoon tea and what an pleasant experience it was. I waited about five minutes for them to setup before taking my seat. Presented with a menu and the months tea selections, I ordered the four course afternoon tea selection with bottomless tea. I had salted caramel pureh tea and something with apricot. The finger sandwiches are AMAZING! As are the scones and dressings. They're not open on Tuesday or Wednesday, but if you can catch them when they are open, they have a wide range of tea and tea related items to peruse as well.<//review>

<username>Katherine Rubie< /username><Time>1583980201596</Time>< Rate>
3</Rate>
< review>
Lines are often long and you have to visit multiple windows - all of which you have to wait for.

Every department is completely separate from each other, which only complicates getting business taken care of (for example, you cannot update your driver's license and registration at the same time, which means you could be there all day waiting to do each thing).

Though parking and entrance is handicapped accessible, they are not handicapped friendly - the chairs in the front row are marked for handicapped people, but everyone else sits in them too; and even though there are desks designed for handicapped service there is no guarantee that a disabled person will be called to that window, while the general population is still served at those desks.

The employees are a mixed bag of very friendly to very rude.

The positive here is that the parking lot appears to have more parking than the Fremont DMV, and the lines are shorter here than the Fremont location.</review>

< Review>
I was in and out of there in less than an hour, no drama. I had done a renewal/RealID, had an appointment, and filled out the application online. Parking was full, but a car pulled out as I entered the lot.

Bring cash or checkbook just in case. My debit card for some reason did not work on their machine, so i had to pay cash for the fees. Get an appointment and fill out your application online if you can, and have your documents ready.

There is a separate line for appointments-only, inside the building. So if you see a line out the door this is likely for the non-appointment. Go inside to check the line for the appointments-only.</Review>
